1. *Reliability:*
   - We prioritize reliability in all aspects of our trips, ensuring that you can trust us to provide a seamless and enjoyable experience.
   - We have a proven track record of organizing successful trips, with a strong emphasis on customer satisfaction.

2. *Safety:*
   - Your safety is our top priority. We do not allow alcohol or smoking during the trip, creating a safe and comfortable environment for all participants, especially women and girls.
   - Our experienced team is well-prepared to handle any unforeseen circumstances and emergencies, ensuring your safety throughout the journey.

3. *Experienced Core Team:*
   - Our core team comprises seasoned travel professionals who have extensive knowledge and experience in organizing and leading trips.
   - Their expertise ensures that your journey is well-planned, smooth, and enjoyable.

4. *Backup Plans:*
   - We understand that travel plans can change due to unforeseen circumstances. Therefore, we always have backup plans in place to adapt to any unexpected situations.
   - This flexibility ensures that your trip continues smoothly, even if there are last-minute changes.

5. *Friendly Trip Leads:*
   - Our trip leads are not just leaders but also friendly companions. They are approachable and committed to making your trip enjoyable.
   - They are there to provide guidance, answer your questions, and ensure that you have a memorable experience.

6. *Transparent Pricing:*
   - Unlike some other companies, we do not add hidden charges. Our pricing is transparent, so you can budget confidently for your trip.
   - We believe in providing value for money without any unpleasant surprises.

7. *Alcohol and Smoking Policies:*
   - Our strict policies against alcohol and smoking during the trip create a respectful and comfortable atmosphere for all participants.
   - This approach promotes a more inclusive and enjoyable experience for everyone.
   - We are not like other companies that permit alcohol during the trip, which can often lead to the destruction of your weekend getaway and, in some unfortunate cases, even turn it into a potentially dangerous experience."

8. *Customer-Centric Approach:*
   - We prioritize your needs and preferences, striving to tailor our trips to your expectations.
   - Your feedback is important to us, and we continuously work to enhance our services based on customer input.

9. *Community and Networking:*
   - Joining Meet Over the Weekend offers you the opportunity to meet like-minded travelers, make new friends, and expand your network.
   - Our trips often lead to lasting connections and memorable experiences.


at Meet Over the Weekend, we are dedicated to providing you with safe, enjoyable, and memorable weekend trips that set us apart from the rest.

Why Late ? Call us now and book your Trip Now. 

If you're not choosing us, we recommend opting for companies that prioritize extreme safety on their trips over budget considerations. We strongly advocate for everyone to travel often and, most importantly, travel safely.

06/12/23, 7:22â€¯am - Vinay It1: Ohoooo
06/12/23, 11:27â€¯am - Sujan PVPSIT: Certainly! Here's a basic example of a MapReduce program in Java to calculate the total salary for each department in a university. This example assumes that your input data is in the format "department,employee,salary".

```java
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.StringTokenizer;

import org.apache.hadoop.conf.Configuration;
import org.apache.hadoop.fs.Path;
import org.apache.hadoop.io.FloatWritable;
import org.apache.hadoop.io.Text;
import org.apache.hadoop.mapreduce.Job;
import org.apache.hadoop.mapreduce.Mapper;
import org.apache.hadoop.mapreduce.Reducer;
import org.apache.hadoop.mapreduce.lib.input.FileInputFormat;
import org.apache.hadoop.mapreduce.lib.output.FileOutputFormat;

public class DepartmentSalary {

    public static class SalaryMapper extends Mapper<Object, Text, Text, FloatWritable> {

        private final static FloatWritable salary = new FloatWritable();
        private Text department = new Text();

        public void map(Object key, Text value, Context context) throws IOException, InterruptedException {
            String[] tokens = value.toString().split(",");
            department.set(tokens[0]);
            salary.set(Float.parseFloat(tokens[2]));
            context.write(department, salary);
        }
    }

    public static class SalaryReducer extends Reducer<Text, FloatWritable, Text, FloatWritable> {

        private FloatWritable result = new FloatWritable();

        public void reduce(Text key, Iterable<FloatWritable> values, Context context)
                throws IOException, InterruptedException {
            float totalSalary = 0;
            for (FloatWritable val : values) {
                totalSalary += val.get();
            }
            result.set(totalSalary);
            context.write(key, result);
        }
    }

    public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception {
        Configuration conf = new Configuration();
        Job job = Job.getInstance(conf, "department salary calculation");
        job.setJarByClass(DepartmentSalary.class);
        job.setMapperClass(SalaryMapper.class);
        job.setReducerClass(SalaryReducer.class);
        job.setOutputKeyClass(Text.class);
        job.setOutputValueClass(FloatWritable.class);
        FileInputFormat.addInputPath(job, new Path(args[0]));
        FileOutputFormat.setOutputPath(job, new Path(args[1]));
        System.exit(job.waitForCompletion(true) ? 0 : 1);
    }
}
```

Make sure to adjust the input and output paths in the `main` method when running the MapReduce job. This is a basic example, and in a real-world scenario, you may need to handle more complex input formats and adapt the code accordingly.

q=[]
for i in range(n):
  a=list(map(int,input().split()))
  q.append(a)
d=int(input())
p=[]
for i in range(n):
  x=list(map(int,input().split()))
  p.append(x)
s=int(input())
real=0
unreal=0
for i in range(n):
  if(q[i][1]<=s and q[i][2]<=s and q[i][2]!=0):
    real+=(p[i][q[i][2]-1]-p[i][q[i][1]-1])*q[i][0]
  elif(q[i][1]>s):
    continue
  else:
    unreal+=(p[i][s-1]-p[i][q[i][1]-1])*q[i][0]
print(real)
print(unreal,end="")

13/12/23, 10:29â€¯am - Sujan PVPSIT: The Management Information System (MIS) has a significant impact on an organization's functions, performance, and productivity:

1. **Efficient Function Management:** MIS enhances the management of marketing, finance, production, and personnel, making it more efficient. It simplifies tracking and monitoring of functional targets.

2. **Exceptional Situations Management:** MIS alerts managers to exceptional situations, prompting timely actions. A disciplined reporting system creates a structured database and knowledge base, saving managers valuable time through readily usable information.

3. **Business Understanding:** MIS contributes to a better understanding of the business by starting with defining data entities and attributes. It utilizes a data dictionary designed for information generation in the organization.

4. **Systemization of Operations:** MIS requires systemizing business operations for effective system design. While this streamlines operations, it also complicates system design. However, this complexity improves overall business administration by instilling discipline in operations.

5. **Alignment with Corporate Goals:** The goals and objectives of MIS align with business goals, indirectly guiding the entire organization toward corporate goals and objectives.

6. **Enhanced Managerial Performance:** MIS positively impacts managerial ability, significantly improving decision-making skills.

7. **Automation of Clerical Work:** By working on basic systems like transaction processing and databases, MIS automates clerical work, relieving human minds for more meaningful tasks.

19/12/23, 10:19â€¯am - Sujan PVPSIT: Day 1 - Pick up from Goa Airport
Pickup from goa Airport/Railway Station and drive to Hotel. On arrive and Check in to Hotel.

Day 2 - Sightseeing of Goa. (NORTH GOA)
Today morning after breakfast leave for the day. & overnight stay at hotel. SEIGHT SEEING TOUR: NORTH GOA 1. Calangute Beach: Widely known as Queen of Goa Beaches. Here Holidays and beat shows draw hundreds of people. 2. Vagator Beach: A beach famous for its seclusion with the Chapora Fort as its imposing backdrop. 3. Anjuna Beach: very popular among the foreigners and is beautiful Picnic spot. 4. Fort Aguada: Built by the Portuguese in 1609-1612 to command the Entry into the river Mondovi in order to protect old Goa for enemy Attack. Fort houses presently the Central jail. A lighthouse is situated nearby.

Day 3 - Sightseeing of Goa. (SOUTH GOA)
SEIGHT SEEING TOUR: SOUTH GOA 1. Miramar Beach: A lovely golden beach of soft sand girdled with palm rees facing the blue Arabian Sea is the capital of Goa, Panajim. Here lies the Samadhi of Goas first Chief Minister. 2. Dona Paula, an idyllic picturesque spot. Command a fine view of Zuari River and Marmagoa harbor. Water scooter facilities are Available here. 3. Bom Jesus of Basilica: (Old Goa Church) Built in 16th Century is the Most famous church in Goa. The mortal remains of St. Francis Xavier, Kept in the Silver casket, are enriched here. 4. Mangueshi Temple: Dedicated to lord Shiva, being built in the 17th Century.

Day 4 - Drop Bus station/ Airport
After breakfast and drop Goa Airport/Railway Station.
